TEST001
  For the Gregorian calendar,
  for a given year, compute the day and month of Easter.
  EASTER_DS uses Duffett-Smith's algorithm.
  EASTER_EGR uses Richards's algorithm.
  EASTER_EGR2 uses Richards's algorithm 2.
  EASTER_KNUTH uses Knuth's algorithm.
  EASTER_STEWART uses Stewart's algorithm.

TEST46
  For the current time and date, "NOW", \n  NOW_TO_JED returns the JED,
  NOW_TO_YJF_COMMON the YJF date,
  NOW_TO_YMDF_COMMON returns the YMDF date,
  NOW_TO_YMDHMS_COMMON the YMDHMS date.

  "NOW" is 23-Apr-2013 22:35:32

  NOW_TO_JED_COMMON:    Now is:   2456406.4
  NOW_TO_YJF_COMMON:    Now is: CE 2013/113.94
  NOW_TO_YMDF_COMMON:   Now is: CE 2013/04/23.94
  NOW_TO_YMDHMS_COMMON: Now is: CE 2013/04/23 22:35:32

  8/8/88
  d/m/yy

    88   8   8

  4 7
  d m

     0   7   4

  On day 1 of month 3 of year 1945
  xx xxx d xx xxxxx m xx xxxx yyyy

  1945   3   1

CALPAK_TEST49

  YYYY-MM-DD-hh-mm-ss

  1999/10/31  14:59:47

  8:30, 01 April 2004
  h:mm, DD NNNNN YYYY

  2004/04/01  08:30:00
